FILE: lib\features\planner\services\spray_conditions_service.dart
------------------------------------------------------------

import 'dart:convert';

import 'package:http/http.dart' as http;

enum SpraySuitability { good, caution, noSpray }

class SprayConditions {
  const SprayConditions({
    required this.temperatureC,
    required this.relativeHumidity,
    required this.windSpeedKmh,
    required this.windGustKmh,
    required this.precipitationMm,
    required this.uvIndex,
    required this.weatherCode,
    required this.updatedAt,
  });

  final double temperatureC;
  final int relativeHumidity;
  final double windSpeedKmh;
  final double windGustKmh;
  final double precipitationMm;
  final double uvIndex;
  final int weatherCode;
  final DateTime updatedAt;

  SpraySuitability get suitability {
    if (precipitationMm > 0.2) return SpraySuitability.noSpray;
    if (windSpeedKmh >= 18 || windGustKmh >= 28) {
      return SpraySuitability.noSpray;
    }
    if (uvIndex >= 8) return SpraySuitability.noSpray;
    if (temperatureC >= 29) return SpraySuitability.noSpray;

    if (windSpeedKmh >= 12 || windGustKmh >= 20) {
      return SpraySuitability.caution;
    }
    if (relativeHumidity >= 90) return SpraySuitability.caution;
    if (relativeHumidity <= 35) return SpraySuitability.caution;
    if (uvIndex >= 6) return SpraySuitability.caution;
    if (temperatureC >= 25) return SpraySuitability.caution;

    return SpraySuitability.good;
  }

  String get conditionLabel {
    if (precipitationMm > 0.2) return 'Rain';
    if (weatherCode == 0) return 'Clear';
    if (weatherCode == 1 || weatherCode == 2 || weatherCode == 3) {
      return 'Cloud';
    }
    if (weatherCode == 45 || weatherCode == 48) return 'Fog';
    if (weatherCode >= 51 && weatherCode <= 67) return 'Rain';
    if (weatherCode >= 71 && weatherCode <= 77) return 'Snow';
    if (weatherCode >= 80 && weatherCode <= 82) return 'Showers';
    if (weatherCode >= 95) return 'Storm';
    return 'Weather';
  }

  String get recommendation {
    switch (suitability) {
      case SpraySuitability.good:
        return 'Good spray window. Conditions are calm and dry.';
      case SpraySuitability.caution:
        return 'Spray with caution. Check wind, humidity, heat, and label limits.';
      case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
        return 'Do not spray now. Conditions are outside safe spray limits.';
    }
  }
}

class SprayConditionsService {
  const SprayConditionsService();

  static const double defaultLatitude = -41.5134;
  static const double defaultLongitude = 173.9612;

  Future<SprayConditions> fetchCurrent({
    double latitude = defaultLatitude,
    double longitude = defaultLongitude,
  }) async {
    final uri = Uri.https('api.open-meteo.com', '/v1/forecast', {
      'latitude': latitude.toString(),
      'longitude': longitude.toString(),
      'current':
          'temperature_2m,relative_humidity_2m,precipitation,weather_code,wind_speed_10m,wind_gusts_10m,uv_index',
      'wind_speed_unit': 'kmh',
      'timezone': 'auto',
      'forecast_days': '1',
    });

    final response = await http.get(uri);

    if (response.statusCode < 200 || response.statusCode >= 300) {
      throw Exception('Spray weather request failed: ${response.statusCode}');
    }

    final decoded = jsonDecode(response.body);

    if (decoded is! Map<String, dynamic>) {
      throw Exception('Invalid spray weather response.');
    }

    final current = decoded['current'];

    if (current is! Map<String, dynamic>) {
      throw Exception('Spray weather response missing current conditions.');
    }

    final timeText = current['time']?.toString();
    final updatedAt = DateTime.tryParse(timeText ?? '') ?? DateTime.now();

    return SprayConditions(
      temperatureC: _toDouble(current['temperature_2m']),
      relativeHumidity: _toInt(current['relative_humidity_2m']),
      windSpeedKmh: _toDouble(current['wind_speed_10m']),
      windGustKmh: _toDouble(current['wind_gusts_10m']),
      precipitationMm: _toDouble(current['precipitation']),
      uvIndex: _toDouble(current['uv_index']),
      weatherCode: _toInt(current['weather_code']),
      updatedAt: updatedAt,
    );
  }

  static double _toDouble(Object? value) {
    if (value is num) return value.toDouble();
    if (value is String) return double.tryParse(value) ?? 0;
    return 0;
  }

  static int _toInt(Object? value) {
    if (value is int) return value;
    if (value is num) return value.round();
    if (value is String) return int.tryParse(value) ?? 0;
    return 0;
  }
}


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: lib\features\planner\ui\bed_card.dart
------------------------------------------------------------

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

import '../../../../core/models/bed.dart';
import '../../../../core/models/seed_catalog.dart';
import '../../../../core/models/seedling.dart';
import '../../../../core/models/sow_calendar.dart';
import '../../../../core/theme/garden_theme.dart';

enum SeedlingFilter { active, ready, overdue, transplanted, all }

class SeedlingsView extends StatefulWidget {
  const SeedlingsView({
    super.key,
    required this.seedlings,
    required this.beds,
    required this.onAddSeedling,
    required this.onUpdateSeedling,
    required this.onDeleteSeedling,
    this.onTransplantSeedling,
    this.onOpenMapView,
  });

  final List<Seedling> seedlings;
  final List<Bed> beds;
  final ValueChanged<Seedling> onAddSeedling;
  final void Function(String id, Seedling Function(Seedling seedling) update)
  onUpdateSeedling;
  final ValueChanged<String> onDeleteSeedling;
  final void Function({
    required String seedlingId,
    required String bedId,
    bool addCropBlockToMap,
  })?
  onTransplantSeedling;
  final VoidCallback? onOpenMapView;

  @override
  State<SeedlingsView> createState() => _SeedlingsViewState();
}

class _SeedlingsViewState extends State<SeedlingsView> {
  SeedlingFilter filter = SeedlingFilter.active;
  bool showPlantNow = true;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final filtered = _filteredSeedlings();
    final plan = SowCalendar.planFor(DateTime.now());

    return Container(
      color: GardenTheme.cream,
      child: CustomScrollView(
        slivers: [
          SliverToBoxAdapter(
            child: _SeedlingsHeader(
              total: widget.seedlings.length,
              active: widget.seedlings.where((s) => !s.isTransplanted).length,
              ready: widget.seedlings.where(_isReady).length,
              overdue: widget.seedlings.where(_isOverdue).length,
              filter: filter,
              showPlantNow: showPlantNow,
              onFilterChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  filter = value;
                });
              },
              onTogglePlantNow: () {
                setState(() {
                  showPlantNow = !showPlantNow;
                });
              },
              onAdd: _openAddDialog,
            ),
          ),
          if (showPlantNow)
            SliverToBoxAdapter(
              child: _PlantNowPanel(
                plan: plan,
                onQuickSow: _quickSow,
                onOpenCatalog: _openAddDialog,
              ),
            ),
          if (filtered.isEmpty)
            SliverFillRemaining(
              hasScrollBody: false,
              child: _EmptySeedlingsState(onAdd: _openAddDialog),
            )
          else
            SliverPadding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
              sliver: SliverLayoutBuilder(
                builder: (context, constraints) {
                  final width = constraints.crossAxisExtent;
                  final columns = width >= 1180
                      ? 3
                      : width >= 760
                      ? 2
                      : 1;

                  return SliverGrid(
                    delegate: SliverChildBuilderDelegate((context, index) {
                      final seedling = filtered[index];

                      return _SeedlingCard(
                        seedling: seedling,
                        bedName: _bedName(seedling.bedId),
                        onEdit: () => _openEditDialog(seedling),
                        onWater: () {
                          widget.onUpdateSeedling(
                            seedling.id,
                            (current) =>
                                current.copyWith(lastWateredAt: DateTime.now()),
                          );
                        },
                        onFeed: () {
                          widget.onUpdateSeedling(
                            seedling.id,
                            (current) =>
                                current.copyWith(lastFedAt: DateTime.now()),
                          );
                        },
                        onTransplant: () => _openTransplantDialog(seedling),
                        onDelete: () {
                          _confirmDelete(seedling);
                        },
                      );
                    }, childCount: filtered.length),
                    gridDelegate: SliverGridDelegateWithFixedCrossAxisCount(
                      crossAxisCount: columns,
                      mainAxisSpacing: 14,
                      crossAxisSpacing: 14,
                      mainAxisExtent: 376,
                    ),
                  );
                },
              ),
            ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  List<Seedling> _filteredSeedlings() {
    final seedlings = [...widget.seedlings]
      ..sort((a, b) => b.sowDate.compareTo(a.sowDate));

    switch (filter) {
      case SeedlingFilter.active:
        return seedlings.where((s) => !s.isTransplanted).toList();
      case SeedlingFilter.ready:
        return seedlings.where(_isReady).toList();
      case SeedlingFilter.overdue:
        return seedlings.where(_isOverdue).toList();
      case SeedlingFilter.transplanted:
        return seedlings.where((s) => s.isTransplanted).toList();
      case SeedlingFilter.all:
        return seedlings;
    }
  }

  bool _isReady(Seedling seedling) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;
    final catalog = SeedCatalog.byKey(seedling.seedKey);
    final age = seedling.daysSinceSowing(DateTime.now());
    return age >= catalog.transplantMinDays;
  }

  bool _isOverdue(Seedling seedling) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;
    final catalog = SeedCatalog.byKey(seedling.seedKey);
    final age = seedling.daysSinceSowing(DateTime.now());
    return age > catalog.transplantMaxDays;
  }

  String _bedName(String? bedId) {
    if (bedId == null || bedId.trim().isEmpty) return 'No bed assigned';

    for (final bed in widget.beds) {
      if (bed.id == bedId) {
        return bed.name.trim().isEmpty ? 'Bed ${bed.number}' : bed.name.trim();
      }
    }

    return 'Missing bed';
  }

  void _quickSow(SowCalendarItem calendarItem) {
    final seed = calendarItem.seed;
    final direct = calendarItem.method == SowMethod.direct;

    widget.onAddSeedling(
      Seedling(
        id: 'seedling-${DateTime.now().microsecondsSinceEpoch}',
        seedKey: seed.key,
        cropName: seed.cropName,
        emoji: seed.emoji,
        category: seed.category,
        variety: '',
        sowDate: DateTime.now(),
        trayType: direct ? 'Direct sow' : 'Tray',
        trayCount: 1,
        location: direct ? 'Garden bed' : 'Seedling area',
        notes: calendarItem.note,
      ),
    );

    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(content: Text('${seed.cropName} added to Seedlings.')),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _openEditDialog(Seedling seedling) async {
    final result = await showDialog<Seedling>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return EditSeedlingDialog(seedling: seedling, beds: widget.beds);
      },
    );

    if (result == null) return;

    widget.onUpdateSeedling(seedling.id, (_) => result);
  }

  Future<void> _openTransplantDialog(Seedling seedling) async {
    if (widget.beds.isEmpty) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(
          content: Text('Add a bed before transplanting seedlings.'),
        ),
      );
      return;
    }

    final result = await showDialog<TransplantSeedlingResult>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return TransplantSeedlingDialogV2(
          seedling: seedling,
          beds: widget.beds,
        );
      },
    );

    if (!mounted) return;

    if (result == null || result.bedId.trim().isEmpty) return;

    final transplant = widget.onTransplantSeedling;

    if (transplant == null) {
      widget.onUpdateSeedling(
        seedling.id,
        (current) => current.copyWith(
          bedId: result.bedId,
          transplantedAt: DateTime.now(),
        ),
      );
    } else {
      transplant(
        seedlingId: seedling.id,
        bedId: result.bedId,
        addCropBlockToMap: result.addCropBlockToMap,
      );
    }

    final bedName = _bedName(result.bedId);

    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text(
          result.addCropBlockToMap
              ? '${seedling.cropName} transplanted to $bedName and added to the map.'
              : '${seedling.cropName} transplanted to $bedName.',
        ),
      ),
    );

    if (result.addCropBlockToMap) {
      widget.onOpenMapView?.call();
    }
  }

  Future<void> _openAddDialog() async {
    final result = await showDialog<Seedling>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return AddSeedlingDialog(beds: widget.beds);
      },
    );

    if (result == null) return;
    widget.onAddSeedling(result);
  }

  Future<void> _confirmDelete(Seedling seedling) async {
    final confirmed = await showDialog<bool>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return AlertDialog(
          backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
          title: const Text('Delete seedling?'),
          content: Text(
            'Delete ${seedling.cropName} from the seedling tracker?',
          ),
          actions: [
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                Navigator.of(context).pop(false);
              },
              child: const Text('Cancel'),
            ),
            FilledButton(
              onPressed: () {
                Navigator.of(context).pop(true);
              },
              child: const Text('Delete'),
            ),
          ],
        );
      },
    );

    if (confirmed == true) {
      widget.onDeleteSeedling(seedling.id);
    }
  }
}

class _SeedlingsHeader extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SeedlingsHeader({
    required this.total,
    required this.active,
    required this.ready,
    required this.overdue,
    required this.filter,
    required this.showPlantNow,
    required this.onFilterChanged,
    required this.onTogglePlantNow,
    required this.onAdd,
  });

  final int total;
  final int active;
  final int ready;
  final int overdue;

                            color: GardenTheme.ink,

                      label: 'Active',
                      value: active.toString(),
                      color: GardenTheme.good,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _HeaderStat(
                      label: 'Ready',
                      value: ready.toString(),
                      color: GardenTheme.warn,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _HeaderStat(
                      label: 'Overdue',
                      value: overdue.toString(),
                      color: GardenTheme.bad,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 14),
                    _FilterButton(
                      label: 'Active',
                      selected: filter == SeedlingFilter.active,
                      onTap: () => onFilterChanged(SeedlingFilter.active),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _FilterButton(
                      label: 'Ready',
                      selected: filter == SeedlingFilter.ready,
                      onTap: () => onFilterChanged(SeedlingFilter.ready),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _FilterButton(
                      label: 'Overdue',
                      selected: filter == SeedlingFilter.overdue,
                      onTap: () => onFilterChanged(SeedlingFilter.overdue),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _FilterButton(
                      label: 'Transplanted',
                      selected: filter == SeedlingFilter.transplanted,
                      onTap: () => onFilterChanged(SeedlingFilter.transplanted),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(width: 8),
                    _FilterButton(
                      label: 'All',
                      selected: filter == SeedlingFilter.all,
                      onTap: () => onFilterChanged(SeedlingFilter.all),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ],
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _PlantNowPanel extends StatelessWidget {
  const _PlantNowPanel({
    required this.plan,
    required this.onQuickSow,
    required this.onOpenCatalog,
  });

  final MonthlySowPlan plan;
  final ValueChanged<SowCalendarItem> onQuickSow;
  final VoidCallback onOpenCatalog;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final nextMonth = plan.month == 12 ? 1 : plan.month + 1;

    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      margin: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(14, 0, 14, 10),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(14),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: GardenTheme.panel,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: LayoutBuilder(
        builder: (context, constraints) {
          final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 920;

          final current = _CalendarColumn(
            title: 'Plant Now',
            subtitle: SowCalendar.monthName(plan.month),
            tray: plan.tray,
            direct: plan.direct,
            either: plan.either,
            emptyText: 'No priority sowing listed for this month.',
            onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
          );

          final next = _CalendarColumn(
            title: 'Prepare Next',
            subtitle: SowCalendar.monthName(nextMonth),
            tray: plan.nextMonthTray,
            direct: plan.nextMonthDirect,
            either: plan.nextMonthEither,
            emptyText: 'No next-month items listed.',
            onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
          );

          if (stacked) {
            return Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                _PlantNowIntro(onOpenCatalog: onOpenCatalog),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                current,
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                next,
              ],
            );
          }

          return Row(
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
            children: [
              Expanded(
                flex: 5,
                child: _PlantNowIntro(onOpenCatalog: onOpenCatalog),
              ),
              const SizedBox(width: 14),
              Expanded(flex: 6, child: current),
              const SizedBox(width: 14),
              Expanded(flex: 5, child: next),
            ],
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _CalendarColumn extends StatelessWidget {
  const _CalendarColumn({
    required this.title,
    required this.subtitle,
    required this.tray,
    required this.direct,
    required this.either,
    required this.emptyText,
    required this.onQuickSow,
  });

  final String title;
  final String subtitle;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> tray;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> direct;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> either;
  final String emptyText;
  final ValueChanged<SowCalendarItem> onQuickSow;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final hasItems = tray.isNotEmpty || direct.isNotEmpty || either.isNotEmpty;

    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(13),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(14),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          Text(
            title.toUpperCase(),
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.muted,
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
              letterSpacing: 1.0,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 3),
          Text(
            subtitle,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.ink,
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 10),
          if (!hasItems)
            Text(
              emptyText,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            )
          else ...[
            if (tray.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Start in trays',
                icon: Icons.inventory_2_outlined,
                items: tray,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
            if (direct.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Direct sow',
                icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                items: direct,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
            if (either.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Tray or direct',
                icon: Icons.compare_arrows,
                items: either,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
          ],
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _CalendarGroup extends StatelessWidget {
  const _CalendarGroup({
    required this.label,
    required this.icon,
    required this.items,
    required this.onQuickSow,
  });

  final String label;
  final IconData icon;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> items;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 10),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          Row(
            children: [
              Icon(icon, color: GardenTheme.muted, size: 15),
              const SizedBox(width: 6),
              Text(
                label.toUpperCase(),
                style: const TextStyle(
                  color: GardenTheme.muted,
                  fontSize: 10,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                  letterSpacing: 0.6,
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 7),
          Wrap(
            spacing: 7,
            runSpacing: 7,
            children: [
              for (final item in items)
                _CalendarSeedChip(
                  item: item,
                  onQuickSow: () => onQuickSow(item),
                ),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 5),
                const Icon(Icons.add, color: GardenTheme.good, size: 13),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _SeedlingCard extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SeedlingCard({
    required this.seedling,
    required this.bedName,
    required this.onWater,
    required this.onFeed,
    required this.onTransplant,
    required this.onEdit,
    required this.onDelete,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final String bedName;
  final VoidCallback onWater;
  final VoidCallback onFeed;
  final VoidCallback onTransplant;
  final VoidCallback onEdit;
  final VoidCallback onDelete;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final catalog = SeedCatalog.byKey(seedling.seedKey);
    final age = seedling.daysSinceSowing(DateTime.now());
    final germinationStart = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.germinationMinDays),
    );
    final germinationEnd = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.germinationMaxDays),
    );
    final transplantStart = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.transplantMinDays),
    );
    final transplantEnd = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.transplantMaxDays),
    );
    final stage = _stageText(seedling, catalog, age);
    final color = _stageColor(seedling, catalog, age);
    final progress = _progress(seedling, catalog, age);

    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: GardenTheme.panel,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        border: Border.all(color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.34)),
      ),
      child: ClipRRect(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(14, 14, 14, 10),
              child: Row(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(seedling.emoji, style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 32)),
                  const SizedBox(width: 10),
                  Expanded(
                    child: Column(
                      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                      children: [
                        Text(
                          seedling.cropName,
                          maxLines: 1,
                          overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                          style: const TextStyle(
                            color: GardenTheme.ink,
                            fontSize: 17,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(height: 3),
                        Text(
                          seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                              ? seedling.category
                              : '${seedling.variety} - ${seedling.category}',
                          maxLines: 1,
                          overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                          style: const TextStyle(
                            color: GardenTheme.muted,
                            fontSize: 12,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(width: 8),
                  _StageBadge(label: stage, color: color),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 14),
              child: ClipRRect(
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(999),
                child: LinearProgressIndicator(
                  value: progress,
                  minHeight: 7,
                  backgroundColor: GardenTheme.paper,
                ),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 10),
            const Divider(height: 1, color: GardenTheme.border),
            Expanded(
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(14),
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(label: 'Age', value: '$age days'),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 8),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(
                            label: 'Sown',
                            value: _shortDate(seedling.sowDate),
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 8),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(
                            label: 'Batch',
                            value: '${seedling.trayCount} ${seedling.trayType}',
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 10),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                      label: 'Germination',
                      value:
                          '${_shortDate(germinationStart)} to ${_shortDate(germinationEnd)}',
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.yard_outlined,
                      label: 'Transplant',
                      value:
                          '${_shortDate(transplantStart)} to ${_shortDate(transplantEnd)}',
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.place_outlined,
                      label: 'Location',
                      value: seedling.location.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Seedling area'
                          : seedling.location.trim(),
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.grid_view_outlined,
                      label: 'Bed',
                      value: bedName,
                    ),
                    const Spacer(),
                    Row(
                      children: [
                        _MiniAction(
                          icon: Icons.water_drop_outlined,
                          label: 'Water',
                          onTap: onWater,
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 7),
                        _MiniAction(
                          icon: Icons.compost_outlined,
                          label: 'Feed',
                          onTap: onFeed,
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 7),
                        if (!seedling.isTransplanted)
                          _MiniAction(
                            icon: Icons.task_alt,
                            label: 'Transplant',
                            onTap: onTransplant,
                          ),
                        const Spacer(),
                        IconButton(
                          tooltip: 'Edit seedling',
                          onPressed: onEdit,
                          icon: const Icon(Icons.edit_outlined),
                          color: GardenTheme.ink,
                        ),
                        IconButton(
                          tooltip: 'Delete',
                          onPressed: onDelete,
                          icon: const Icon(Icons.delete_outline),
                          color: GardenTheme.bad,
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  static String _stageText(
    Seedling seedling,
    SeedCatalogItem catalog,
    int age,
  ) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 'Transplanted';
    if (age > catalog.transplantMaxDays) return 'Overdue';
    if (age >= catalog.transplantMinDays) return 'Ready';
    if (age >= catalog.germinationMinDays) return 'Germinating';
    return 'Waiting';
  }

  static Color _stageColor(
    Seedling seedling,
    SeedCatalogItem catalog,
    int age,
  ) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return GardenTheme.good;
    if (age > catalog.transplantMaxDays) return GardenTheme.bad;
    if (age >= catalog.transplantMinDays) return GardenTheme.warn;
    if (age >= catalog.germinationMinDays) return GardenTheme.good;
    return GardenTheme.muted;
  }

  static double _progress(Seedling seedling, SeedCatalogItem catalog, int age) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 1;

    final target = catalog.transplantMaxDays;
    if (target <= 0) return 0;

    return (age / target).clamp(0, 1).toDouble();
  }
}

class _StageBadge extends StatelessWidget {
  const _StageBadge({required this.label, required this.color});

  final String label;
  final Color color;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 112),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 9, vertical: 5),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.12),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(999),
        border: Border.all(color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.28)),
      ),
      child: Text(
        label.toUpperCase(),
        maxLines: 1,
        overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
        style: TextStyle(
          color: color,
          fontSize: 10,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
          letterSpacing: 0.4,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _SeedlingActivityTimeline extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SeedlingActivityTimeline({
    required this.seedling,
    required this.catalog,
    required this.ageDays,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final SeedCatalogItem catalog;
  final int ageDays;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final nextAction = _nextAction();
    final actionColor = _nextActionColor(nextAction);

    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(top: 4),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(10),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: GardenTheme.paper,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          const Text(
            'ACTIVITY',
            maxLines: 1,
            overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
            style: TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.muted,
              fontSize: 9,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
              letterSpacing: 0.8,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 7),
          Wrap(
            spacing: 8,
            runSpacing: 6,
            children: [
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.calendar_today_outlined,
                label: 'Sown',
                value: _shortDate(seedling.sowDate),
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.water_drop_outlined,
                label: 'Watered',
                value: _relativeDate(seedling.lastWateredAt),
                color: _isWaterDue() ? GardenTheme.warn : GardenTheme.good,
              ),
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.compost_outlined,
                label: 'Fed',
                value: _relativeDate(seedling.lastFedAt),
                color: _isFeedDue() ? GardenTheme.warn : GardenTheme.good,
              ),
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                label: 'Germination',
                value:
                    '${catalog.germinationMinDays}-${catalog.germinationMaxDays} days',
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.yard_outlined,
                label: 'Transplant',
                value:
                    '${catalog.transplantMinDays}-${catalog.transplantMaxDays} days',
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityChip(
                icon: Icons.bolt_outlined,
                label: 'Next',
                value: nextAction,
                color: actionColor,
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  bool _isWaterDue() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;

    final lastWateredAt = seedling.lastWateredAt;
    if (lastWateredAt == null) return true;

    return _daysSince(lastWateredAt) >= 2;
  }

  bool _isFeedDue() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;
    if (ageDays < 14) return false;

    final lastFedAt = seedling.lastFedAt;
    if (lastFedAt == null) return true;

    return _daysSince(lastFedAt) >= 10;
  }

  String _nextAction() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 'No action';

    if (ageDays >= catalog.transplantMinDays) {
      return 'Ready to transplant';
    }

    if (_isWaterDue()) return 'Water due';
    if (_isFeedDue()) return 'Feed due';

    return 'No action';
  }

  Color _nextActionColor(String action) {
    switch (action) {
      case 'Ready to transplant':
        return GardenTheme.warn;
      case 'Water due':
        return GardenTheme.warn;
      case 'Feed due':
        return GardenTheme.warn;
      default:
        return GardenTheme.good;
    }
  }
}

class _ActivityChip extends StatelessWidget {
  const _ActivityChip({
    required this.icon,
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    required this.color,
  });

  final IconData icon;
  final String label;
  final String value;
  final Color color;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      constraints: const BoxConstraints(minWidth: 118, maxWidth: 180),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 9, vertical: 7),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          Icon(icon, color: color, size: 14),
          const SizedBox(width: 6),
          Flexible(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  label.toUpperCase(),
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 8,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    letterSpacing: 0.5,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 2),
                Text(
                  value,
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: color,
                    fontSize: 11,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

String _relativeDate(DateTime? date) {
  if (date == null) return 'Never';

  final days = _daysSince(date);

  if (days <= 0) return 'Today';
  if (days == 1) return 'Yesterday';

  return '$days days ago';
}

int _daysSince(DateTime date) {
  final now = DateTime.now();
  final today = DateTime(now.year, now.month, now.day);
  final target = DateTime(date.year, date.month, date.day);

  return today.difference(target).inDays;
}

class AddSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const AddSeedlingDialog({super.key, required this.beds});

  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<AddSeedlingDialog> createState() => _AddSeedlingDialogState();
}

class _AddSeedlingDialogState extends State<AddSeedlingDialog> {
  final formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();

  SeedCatalogItem selected = SeedCatalog.items.first;
  DateTime sowDate = DateTime.now();
  String? selectedBedId;

  late final TextEditingController varietyController;
  late final TextEditingController trayTypeController;
  late final TextEditingController trayCountController;
  late final TextEditingController locationController;
  late final TextEditingController notesController;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    varietyController = TextEditingController();
    trayTypeController = TextEditingController(text: 'Tray');
    trayCountController = TextEditingController(text: '1');
    locationController = TextEditingController(text: 'Seedling area');
    notesController = TextEditingController();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    varietyController.dispose();
    trayTypeController.dispose();
    trayCountController.dispose();
    locationController.dispose();
    notesController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Dialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        side: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: BoxConstraints(
          maxWidth: 620,
          maxHeight: MediaQuery.of(context).size.height * 0.88,
        ),
        child: SingleChildScrollView(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(22),
          child: Form(
            key: formKey,
            child: Column(
              mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                const Text(
                  'Sow Seed',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.ink,
                    fontSize: 24,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    letterSpacing: -0.3,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 6),
                const Text(
                  'Add a seedling batch and track germination plus transplant timing.',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 13,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 18),
                DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                  initialValue: selected.key,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  decoration: _inputDecoration('SEED TYPE'),
                  items: [
                    for (final item in SeedCatalog.items)
                      DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: item.key,
                        child: Text('${item.emoji} ${item.cropName}'),
                      ),
                  ],
                  onChanged: (value) {
                    final key = value ?? selected.key;
                    setState(() {
                      selected = SeedCatalog.byKey(key);
                    });
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Variety',
                  controller: varietyController,
                  hintText: selected.varieties.isEmpty
                      ? 'Optional'
                      : selected.varieties.take(3).join(', '),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [
                          _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    final location = _TextField(
                      label: 'Location',
                      controller: locationController,
                      validator: _required,
                    );

                    final bed = DropdownButtonFormField<String?>(
                      initialValue: selectedBedId,
                      isExpanded: true,
                      decoration: _inputDecoration('ASSIGNED BED'),
                      items: [
                        const DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                          value: null,
                          child: Text('No bed assigned'),
                        ),
                        for (final bed in widget.beds)
                          DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                            value: bed.id,
                            child: Text(
                              bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                                  ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                                  : bed.name.trim(),
                              overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                            ),
                          ),
                      ],
                      onChanged: (value) {
                        setState(() {
                          selectedBedId = value;
                        });
                      },
                    );

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [location, const SizedBox(height: 12), bed],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(child: location),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(child: bed),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Notes',
                  controller: notesController,
                  maxLines: 3,
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 14),
                Container(
                  width: double.infinity,
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: GardenTheme.paper,
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                    border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
                  ),
                  child: Text(
                    '${selected.tip} Germination: ${selected.germinationMinDays}-${selected.germinationMaxDays} days. Transplant: ${selected.transplantMinDays}-${selected.transplantMaxDays} days.',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.muted,
                      fontSize: 12,
                      height: 1.35,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 22),
                Wrap(
                  spacing: 10,
                  runSpacing: 10,
                  alignment: WrapAlignment.end,
                  children: [
                    TextButton(
                      onPressed: () {
                        Navigator.of(context).pop();
                      },
                      child: const Text('Cancel'),
                    ),
                    FilledButton(
                      onPressed: _submit,
                      child: const Text('Sow seed'),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _pickSowDate() async {
    final result = await showDatePicker(
      context: context,
      initialDate: sowDate,
      firstDate: DateTime.now().subtract(const Duration(days: 365)),
      lastDate: DateTime.now().add(const Duration(days: 30)),
    );

    if (result == null) return;

    setState(() {
      sowDate = result;
    });
  }

  void _submit() {
    if (!formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;

    final id = 'seedling-${DateTime.now().microsecondsSinceEpoch}';

    Navigator.of(context).pop(
      Seedling(
        id: id,
        seedKey: selected.key,
        cropName: selected.cropName,
        emoji: selected.emoji,
        category: selected.category,
        variety: varietyController.text.trim(),
        sowDate: sowDate,
        trayType: trayTypeController.text.trim(),
        trayCount: int.tryParse(trayCountController.text.trim()) ?? 1,
        location: locationController.text.trim(),
        notes: notesController.text.trim(),
        bedId: selectedBedId,
      ),
    );
  }

  String? _required(String? value) {
    if (value == null || value.trim().isEmpty) {
      return 'Required';
    }
    return null;
  }

  String? _positiveInt(String? value) {
    final parsed = int.tryParse(value ?? '');
    if (parsed == null) return 'Enter a number';
    if (parsed < 1) return 'Minimum 1';
    return null;
  }
}

class _TextField extends StatelessWidget {
  const _TextField({
    required this.label,
    required this.controller,
    this.hintText,
    this.keyboardType,
    this.validator,
    this.maxLines = 1,
  });

  final String label;
  final TextEditingController controller;
  final String? hintText;
  final TextInputType? keyboardType;
  final String? Function(String?)? validator;
  final int maxLines;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return TextFormField(
      controller: controller,
      keyboardType: keyboardType,
      validator: validator,
      maxLines: maxLines,
      style: const TextStyle(
        color: GardenTheme.ink,
        fontSize: 14,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
      ),
      decoration: _inputDecoration(label, hintText: hintText),
    );
  }
}

class _DateButton extends StatelessWidget {
  const _DateButton({
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  final String label;
  final String value;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return InkWell(
      onTap: onTap,
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      child: InputDecorator(
        decoration: _inputDecoration(label),
        child: Text(
          value,
          style: const TextStyle(
            color: GardenTheme.ink,
            fontSize: 14,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

InputDecoration _inputDecoration(String label, {String? hintText}) {
  return InputDecoration(
    labelText: label.toUpperCase(),
    hintText: hintText,
    labelStyle: const TextStyle(
      color: GardenTheme.muted,
      fontSize: 11,
      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
      letterSpacing: 0.8,
    ),
    filled: true,
    fillColor: GardenTheme.paper,
    contentPadding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 12),
    enabledBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.border),
    ),
    focusedBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.ink, width: 1.4),
    ),
    errorBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.bad),
    ),
    focusedErrorBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.bad, width: 1.4),
    ),
  );
}

String _shortDate(DateTime date) {
  return '${date.day.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}/${date.month.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
}

class EditSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const EditSeedlingDialog({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

}

                  'Update crop, sow date, batch details, location, bed assignment, and notes.',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 13,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 18),
                DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                  initialValue: selected.key,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  decoration: _inputDecoration('SEED TYPE'),
                  items: [
                    for (final item in SeedCatalog.items)
                      DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: item.key,
                        child: Text('${item.emoji} ${item.cropName}'),
                      ),
                  ],
                  onChanged: (value) {
                    final key = value ?? selected.key;
                    setState(() {
                      selected = SeedCatalog.byKey(key);
                    });
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Variety',
                  controller: varietyController,
                  hintText: selected.varieties.isEmpty
                      ? 'Optional'
                      : selected.varieties.take(3).join(', '),

                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    final location = _TextField(
                      label: 'Location',
                      controller: locationController,
                      validator: _required,
                    );

                    final bed = DropdownButtonFormField<String?>(
                      initialValue: selectedBedId,
                      isExpanded: true,
                      decoration: _inputDecoration('ASSIGNED BED'),
                      items: [
                        const DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                          value: null,
                          child: Text('No bed assigned'),
                        ),
                        for (final bed in widget.beds)
                          DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                            value: bed.id,
                            child: Text(
                              bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                                  ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                                  : bed.name.trim(),
                              overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                            ),
                          ),
                      ],
                      onChanged: (value) {
                        setState(() {
                          selectedBedId = value;
                        });
                      },
                    );

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [location, const SizedBox(height: 12), bed],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(child: location),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(child: bed),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Notes',
                  controller: notesController,
                  maxLines: 3,
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 14),
                Container(
                  width: double.infinity,
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: GardenTheme.paper,
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                    border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
                  ),
                  child: Text(
                    '${selected.tip} Germination: ${selected.germinationMinDays}-${selected.germinationMaxDays} days. Transplant: ${selected.transplantMinDays}-${selected.transplantMaxDays} days.',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.muted,
                      fontSize: 12,
                      height: 1.35,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 22),
                Wrap(
                  spacing: 10,
                  runSpacing: 10,
                  alignment: WrapAlignment.end,
                  children: [
                    TextButton(
                      onPressed: () {
                        Navigator.of(context).pop();
                      },
                      child: const Text('Cancel'),
                    ),
                    FilledButton(
                      onPressed: _submit,
                      child: const Text('Save changes'),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _pickSowDate() async {
    final result = await showDatePicker(
      context: context,
      initialDate: sowDate,
      firstDate: DateTime.now().subtract(const Duration(days: 365)),
      lastDate: DateTime.now().add(const Duration(days: 30)),
    );

    if (result == null) return;

    setState(() {
      sowDate = result;
    });
  }

  void _submit() {
    if (!formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;

    Navigator.of(context).pop(
      Seedling(
        id: widget.seedling.id,
        seedKey: selected.key,
        cropName: selected.cropName,
        emoji: selected.emoji,
        category: selected.category,
        variety: varietyController.text.trim(),
        sowDate: sowDate,
        trayType: trayTypeController.text.trim(),
        trayCount: int.tryParse(trayCountController.text.trim()) ?? 1,
        location: locationController.text.trim(),
        notes: notesController.text.trim(),
        bedId: selectedBedId,
        lastWateredAt: widget.seedling.lastWateredAt,
        lastFedAt: widget.seedling.lastFedAt,
        transplantedAt: widget.seedling.transplantedAt,
      ),
    );
  }

  String? _required(String? value) {
    if (value == null || value.trim().isEmpty) {
      return 'Required';
    }

    return null;
  }

  String? _positiveInt(String? value) {
    final parsed = int.tryParse(value ?? '');

    if (parsed == null) return 'Enter a number';
    if (parsed < 1) return 'Minimum 1';

    return null;
  }
}

class TransplantSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const TransplantSeedlingDialog({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<TransplantSeedlingDialog> createState() =>
      _TransplantSeedlingDialogState();
}

class _TransplantSeedlingDialogState extends State<TransplantSeedlingDialog> {
  String? selectedBedId;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    final existingBedId = widget.seedling.bedId;

    if (existingBedId != null &&
        widget.beds.any((bed) => bed.id == existingBedId)) {
      selectedBedId = existingBedId;
    } else if (widget.beds.isNotEmpty) {
      selectedBedId = widget.beds.first.id;
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AlertDialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      title: const Text('Transplant to Bed'),
      content: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 460),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Row(
              children: [
                Text(
                  widget.seedling.emoji,
                  style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 30),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 10),
                Expanded(
                  child: Text(
                    widget.seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                        ? widget.seedling.cropName
                        : '${widget.seedling.cropName} - ${widget.seedling.variety}',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.ink,
                      fontSize: 16,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            const Text(
              'Choose the bed this seedling was transplanted into. The crop name will be added to that bed if it is not already listed.',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                height: 1.35,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              initialValue: selectedBedId,
              isExpanded: true,
              decoration: _inputDecoration('TARGET BED'),
              items: [
                for (final bed in widget.beds)
                  DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                    value: bed.id,
                    child: Text(
                      bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                          : '${bed.name} (${bed.zone})',
                      overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                    ),
                  ),
              ],
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedBedId = value;
                });
              },
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      actions: [
        TextButton(
          onPressed: () {
            Navigator.of(context).pop();
          },
          child: const Text('Cancel'),
        ),
        FilledButton.icon(
          onPressed: selectedBedId == null
              ? null
              : () {
                  Navigator.of(context).pop(selectedBedId);
                },
          icon: const Icon(Icons.task_alt),
          label: const Text('Transplant'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

class TransplantSeedlingResult {
  const TransplantSeedlingResult({
    required this.bedId,
    required this.addCropBlockToMap,
  });

  final String bedId;
  final bool addCropBlockToMap;
}

class TransplantSeedlingDialogV2 extends StatefulWidget {
  const TransplantSeedlingDialogV2({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<TransplantSeedlingDialogV2> createState() =>
      _TransplantSeedlingDialogV2State();
}

class _TransplantSeedlingDialogV2State
    extends State<TransplantSeedlingDialogV2> {
  String? selectedBedId;
  bool addCropBlockToMap = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    final existingBedId = widget.seedling.bedId;

    if (existingBedId != null &&
        widget.beds.any((bed) => bed.id == existingBedId)) {
      selectedBedId = existingBedId;
    } else if (widget.beds.isNotEmpty) {
      selectedBedId = widget.beds.first.id;
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AlertDialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      title: const Text('Transplant to Bed'),
      content: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 480),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Row(
              children: [
                Text(
                  widget.seedling.emoji,
                  style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 30),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 10),
                Expanded(
                  child: Text(
                    widget.seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                        ? widget.seedling.cropName
                        : '${widget.seedling.cropName} - ${widget.seedling.variety}',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.ink,
                      fontSize: 16,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            const Text(
              'Choose the bed this seedling was transplanted into. The crop name will be added to that bed. If map placement is enabled, a crop block will be added inside the bed on the map.',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                height: 1.35,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              initialValue: selectedBedId,
              isExpanded: true,
              decoration: _inputDecoration('TARGET BED'),
              items: [
                for (final bed in widget.beds)
                  DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                    value: bed.id,
                    child: Text(
                      bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                          : '${bed.name} (${bed.zone})',
                      overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                    ),
                  ),
              ],
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedBedId = value;
                });
              },
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 12),
            CheckboxListTile(
              value: addCropBlockToMap,
              dense: true,
              contentPadding: EdgeInsets.zero,
              controlAffinity: ListTileControlAffinity.leading,
              title: const Text(
                'Add crop block to map',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: GardenTheme.ink,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
                ),
              ),
              subtitle: const Text(
                'Creates a visible crop row/block inside the selected bed.',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: GardenTheme.muted,
                  fontSize: 12,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                ),
              ),
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  addCropBlockToMap = value ?? true;
                });
              },
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      actions: [
        TextButton(
          onPressed: () {
            Navigator.of(context).pop();
          },
          child: const Text('Cancel'),
        ),
        FilledButton.icon(
          onPressed: selectedBedId == null
              ? null
              : () {
                  Navigator.of(context).pop(
                    TransplantSeedlingResult(
                      bedId: selectedBedId!,
                      addCropBlockToMap: addCropBlockToMap,
                    ),
                  );
                },
          icon: const Icon(Icons.task_alt),
          label: const Text('Transplant'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: lib\features\planner\ui\garden_screen.dart
