class _CalendarColumn extends StatelessWidget {
  const _CalendarColumn({
    required this.title,
    required this.subtitle,
    required this.tray,
    required this.direct,
    required this.either,
    required this.emptyText,
    required this.onQuickSow,
  });

  final String title;
  final String subtitle;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> tray;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> direct;
  final List<SowCalendarItem> either;
  final String emptyText;
  final ValueChanged<SowCalendarItem> onQuickSow;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final hasItems = tray.isNotEmpty || direct.isNotEmpty || either.isNotEmpty;

    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(13),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(14),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          Text(
            title.toUpperCase(),
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.muted,
              fontSize: 10,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
              letterSpacing: 1.0,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 3),
          Text(
            subtitle,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.ink,
              fontSize: 18,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 10),
          if (!hasItems)
            Text(
              emptyText,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            )
          else ...[
            if (tray.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Start in trays',
                icon: Icons.inventory_2_outlined,
                items: tray,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
            if (direct.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Direct sow',
                icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                items: direct,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
            if (either.isNotEmpty)
              _CalendarGroup(
                label: 'Tray or direct',
                icon: Icons.compare_arrows,
                items: either,
                onQuickSow: onQuickSow,
              ),
          ],
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _SeedlingCard extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SeedlingCard({
    required this.seedling,
    required this.bedName,
    required this.onWater,
    required this.onFeed,
    required this.onTransplant,
    required this.onEdit,
    required this.onDelete,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final String bedName;
  final VoidCallback onWater;
  final VoidCallback onFeed;
  final VoidCallback onTransplant;
  final VoidCallback onEdit;
  final VoidCallback onDelete;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final catalog = SeedCatalog.byKey(seedling.seedKey);
    final age = seedling.daysSinceSowing(DateTime.now());
    final germinationStart = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.germinationMinDays),
    );
    final germinationEnd = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.germinationMaxDays),
    );
    final transplantStart = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.transplantMinDays),
    );
    final transplantEnd = seedling.sowDate.add(
      Duration(days: catalog.transplantMaxDays),
    );
    final stage = _stageText(seedling, catalog, age);
    final color = _stageColor(seedling, catalog, age);
    final progress = _progress(seedling, catalog, age);

    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: GardenTheme.panel,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        border: Border.all(color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.34)),
      ),
      child: ClipRRect(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(14, 14, 14, 10),
              child: Row(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(seedling.emoji, style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 32)),
                  const SizedBox(width: 10),
                  Expanded(
                    child: Column(
                      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                      children: [
                        Text(
                          seedling.cropName,
                          maxLines: 1,
                          overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                          style: const TextStyle(
                            color: GardenTheme.ink,
                            fontSize: 17,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(height: 3),
                        Text(
                          seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                              ? seedling.category
                              : '${seedling.variety} - ${seedling.category}',
                          maxLines: 1,
                          overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                          style: const TextStyle(
                            color: GardenTheme.muted,
                            fontSize: 12,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(width: 8),
                  _StageBadge(label: stage, color: color),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 14),
              child: ClipRRect(
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(999),
                child: LinearProgressIndicator(
                  value: progress,
                  minHeight: 7,
                  backgroundColor: GardenTheme.paper,
                ),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 10),
            const Divider(height: 1, color: GardenTheme.border),
            Expanded(
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.all(14),
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(label: 'Age', value: '$age days'),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 8),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(
                            label: 'Sown',
                            value: _shortDate(seedling.sowDate),
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 8),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _FactBox(
                            label: 'Batch',
                            value: '${seedling.trayCount} ${seedling.trayType}',
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 10),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                      label: 'Germination',
                      value:
                          '${_shortDate(germinationStart)} to ${_shortDate(germinationEnd)}',
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.yard_outlined,
                      label: 'Transplant',
                      value:
                          '${_shortDate(transplantStart)} to ${_shortDate(transplantEnd)}',
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.place_outlined,
                      label: 'Location',
                      value: seedling.location.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Seedling area'
                          : seedling.location.trim(),
                    ),
                    _TimelineRow(
                      icon: Icons.grid_view_outlined,
                      label: 'Bed',
                      value: bedName,
                    ),

                    _SeedlingActivitySummary(
                      seedling: seedling,
                      catalog: catalog,
                      ageDays: age,
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 8),
                    const Spacer(),
                    Row(
                      children: [
                        _MiniAction(
                          icon: Icons.water_drop_outlined,
                          label: 'Water',
                          onTap: onWater,
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 7),
                        _MiniAction(
                          icon: Icons.compost_outlined,
                          label: 'Feed',
                          onTap: onFeed,
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 7),
                        if (!seedling.isTransplanted)
                          _MiniAction(
                            icon: Icons.task_alt,
                            label: 'Transplant',
                            onTap: onTransplant,
                          ),
                        const Spacer(),
                        IconButton(
                          tooltip: 'Edit seedling',
                          onPressed: onEdit,
                          icon: const Icon(Icons.edit_outlined),
                          color: GardenTheme.ink,
                        ),
                        IconButton(
                          tooltip: 'Delete',
                          onPressed: onDelete,
                          icon: const Icon(Icons.delete_outline),
                          color: GardenTheme.bad,
                        ),
                      ],
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  static String _stageText(
    Seedling seedling,
    SeedCatalogItem catalog,
    int age,
  ) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 'Transplanted';
    if (age > catalog.transplantMaxDays) return 'Overdue';
    if (age >= catalog.transplantMinDays) return 'Ready';
    if (age >= catalog.germinationMinDays) return 'Germinating';
    return 'Waiting';
  }

  static Color _stageColor(
    Seedling seedling,
    SeedCatalogItem catalog,
    int age,
  ) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return GardenTheme.good;
    if (age > catalog.transplantMaxDays) return GardenTheme.bad;
    if (age >= catalog.transplantMinDays) return GardenTheme.warn;
    if (age >= catalog.germinationMinDays) return GardenTheme.good;
    return GardenTheme.muted;
  }

  static double _progress(Seedling seedling, SeedCatalogItem catalog, int age) {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 1;

    final target = catalog.transplantMaxDays;
    if (target <= 0) return 0;

    return (age / target).clamp(0, 1).toDouble();
  }
}

class _SeedlingActivitySummary extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SeedlingActivitySummary({
    required this.seedling,
    required this.catalog,
    required this.ageDays,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final SeedCatalogItem catalog;
  final int ageDays;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final nextAction = _nextAction();
    final nextActionColor = _nextActionColor(nextAction);

    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      margin: const EdgeInsets.only(top: 4),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(10),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: GardenTheme.paper,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Column(
        crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
        children: [
          const Text(
            'ACTIVITY',
            maxLines: 1,
            overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
            style: TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.muted,
              fontSize: 9,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
              letterSpacing: 0.8,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          Wrap(
            spacing: 7,
            runSpacing: 7,
            children: [
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Sown',
                value: _shortDate(seedling.sowDate),
                icon: Icons.calendar_today_outlined,
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Watered',
                value: _seedlingRelativeDate(seedling.lastWateredAt),
                icon: Icons.water_drop_outlined,
                color: _isWaterDue() ? GardenTheme.warn : GardenTheme.good,
              ),
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Fed',
                value: _seedlingRelativeDate(seedling.lastFedAt),
                icon: Icons.compost_outlined,
                color: _isFeedDue() ? GardenTheme.warn : GardenTheme.good,
              ),
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Germination',
                value:
                    '${catalog.germinationMinDays}-${catalog.germinationMaxDays} days',
                icon: Icons.grass_outlined,
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Transplant',
                value:
                    '${catalog.transplantMinDays}-${catalog.transplantMaxDays} days',
                icon: Icons.yard_outlined,
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
              ),
              _ActivityPill(
                label: 'Next',
                value: nextAction,
                icon: Icons.bolt_outlined,
                color: nextActionColor,
                wide: true,
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  bool _isWaterDue() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;

    final lastWateredAt = seedling.lastWateredAt;
    if (lastWateredAt == null) return true;

    return _seedlingDaysSince(lastWateredAt) >= 2;
  }

  bool _isFeedDue() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return false;
    if (ageDays < 14) return false;

    final lastFedAt = seedling.lastFedAt;
    if (lastFedAt == null) return true;

    return _seedlingDaysSince(lastFedAt) >= 10;
  }

  String _nextAction() {
    if (seedling.isTransplanted) return 'No action';

    if (ageDays >= catalog.transplantMinDays) {
      return 'Ready to transplant';
    }

    if (_isWaterDue()) return 'Water due';
    if (_isFeedDue()) return 'Feed due';

    return 'No action';
  }

  Color _nextActionColor(String action) {
    switch (action) {
      case 'Ready to transplant':
      case 'Water due':
      case 'Feed due':
        return GardenTheme.warn;
      default:
        return GardenTheme.good;
    }
  }
}

class _ActivityPill extends StatelessWidget {
  const _ActivityPill({
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    required this.icon,
    required this.color,
    this.wide = false,
  });

  final String label;
  final String value;
  final IconData icon;
  final Color color;
  final bool wide;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      width: wide ? 172 : 126,
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 8, vertical: 7),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Icon(icon, color: color, size: 14),
          const SizedBox(width: 6),
          Expanded(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  label.toUpperCase(),
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 8,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    letterSpacing: 0.5,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 2),
                Text(
                  value,
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: color,
                    fontSize: 11,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

String _seedlingRelativeDate(DateTime? date) {
  if (date == null) return 'Never';

  final days = _seedlingDaysSince(date);

  if (days <= 0) return 'Today';
  if (days == 1) return 'Yesterday';

  return '$days days ago';
}

int _seedlingDaysSince(DateTime date) {
  final now = DateTime.now();
  final today = DateTime(now.year, now.month, now.day);
  final target = DateTime(date.year, date.month, date.day);

  return today.difference(target).inDays;
}

class AddSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const AddSeedlingDialog({super.key, required this.beds});

  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<AddSeedlingDialog> createState() => _AddSeedlingDialogState();
}

class _AddSeedlingDialogState extends State<AddSeedlingDialog> {
  final formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();

  SeedCatalogItem selected = SeedCatalog.items.first;
  DateTime sowDate = DateTime.now();
  String? selectedBedId;

  late final TextEditingController varietyController;
  late final TextEditingController trayTypeController;
  late final TextEditingController trayCountController;
  late final TextEditingController locationController;
  late final TextEditingController notesController;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    varietyController = TextEditingController();
    trayTypeController = TextEditingController(text: 'Tray');
    trayCountController = TextEditingController(text: '1');
    locationController = TextEditingController(text: 'Seedling area');
    notesController = TextEditingController();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    varietyController.dispose();
    trayTypeController.dispose();
    trayCountController.dispose();
    locationController.dispose();
    notesController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Dialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        side: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: BoxConstraints(
          maxWidth: 620,
          maxHeight: MediaQuery.of(context).size.height * 0.88,
        ),
        child: SingleChildScrollView(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(22),
          child: Form(
            key: formKey,
            child: Column(
              mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                const Text(
                  'Sow Seed',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.ink,
                    fontSize: 24,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    letterSpacing: -0.3,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 6),
                const Text(
                  'Add a seedling batch and track germination plus transplant timing.',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 13,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 18),
                DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                  initialValue: selected.key,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  decoration: _inputDecoration('SEED TYPE'),
                  items: [
                    for (final item in SeedCatalog.items)
                      DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: item.key,
                        child: Text('${item.emoji} ${item.cropName}'),
                      ),
                  ],
                  onChanged: (value) {
                    final key = value ?? selected.key;
                    setState(() {
                      selected = SeedCatalog.byKey(key);
                    });
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Variety',
                  controller: varietyController,
                  hintText: selected.varieties.isEmpty
                      ? 'Optional'
                      : selected.varieties.take(3).join(', '),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [
                          _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    final location = _TextField(
                      label: 'Location',
                      controller: locationController,
                      validator: _required,
                    );

                    final bed = DropdownButtonFormField<String?>(
                      initialValue: selectedBedId,
                      isExpanded: true,
                      decoration: _inputDecoration('ASSIGNED BED'),
                      items: [
                        const DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                          value: null,
                          child: Text('No bed assigned'),
                        ),
                        for (final bed in widget.beds)
                          DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                            value: bed.id,
                            child: Text(
                              bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                                  ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                                  : bed.name.trim(),
                              overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                            ),
                          ),
                      ],
                      onChanged: (value) {
                        setState(() {
                          selectedBedId = value;
                        });
                      },
                    );

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [location, const SizedBox(height: 12), bed],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(child: location),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(child: bed),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Notes',
                  controller: notesController,
                  maxLines: 3,
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 14),
                Container(
                  width: double.infinity,
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: GardenTheme.paper,
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                    border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
                  ),
                  child: Text(
                    '${selected.tip} Germination: ${selected.germinationMinDays}-${selected.germinationMaxDays} days. Transplant: ${selected.transplantMinDays}-${selected.transplantMaxDays} days.',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.muted,
                      fontSize: 12,
                      height: 1.35,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 22),
                Wrap(
                  spacing: 10,
                  runSpacing: 10,
                  alignment: WrapAlignment.end,
                  children: [
                    TextButton(
                      onPressed: () {
                        Navigator.of(context).pop();
                      },
                      child: const Text('Cancel'),
                    ),
                    FilledButton(
                      onPressed: _submit,
                      child: const Text('Sow seed'),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _pickSowDate() async {
    final result = await showDatePicker(
      context: context,
      initialDate: sowDate,
      firstDate: DateTime.now().subtract(const Duration(days: 365)),
      lastDate: DateTime.now().add(const Duration(days: 30)),
    );

    if (result == null) return;

    setState(() {
      sowDate = result;
    });
  }

  void _submit() {
    if (!formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;

    final id = 'seedling-${DateTime.now().microsecondsSinceEpoch}';

    Navigator.of(context).pop(
      Seedling(
        id: id,
        seedKey: selected.key,
        cropName: selected.cropName,
        emoji: selected.emoji,
        category: selected.category,
        variety: varietyController.text.trim(),
        sowDate: sowDate,
        trayType: trayTypeController.text.trim(),
        trayCount: int.tryParse(trayCountController.text.trim()) ?? 1,
        location: locationController.text.trim(),
        notes: notesController.text.trim(),
        bedId: selectedBedId,
      ),
    );
  }

  String? _required(String? value) {
    if (value == null || value.trim().isEmpty) {
      return 'Required';
    }
    return null;
  }

  String? _positiveInt(String? value) {
    final parsed = int.tryParse(value ?? '');
    if (parsed == null) return 'Enter a number';
    if (parsed < 1) return 'Minimum 1';
    return null;
  }
}

class _TextField extends StatelessWidget {
  const _TextField({
    required this.label,
    required this.controller,
    this.hintText,
    this.keyboardType,
    this.validator,
    this.maxLines = 1,
  });

  final String label;
  final TextEditingController controller;
  final String? hintText;
  final TextInputType? keyboardType;
  final String? Function(String?)? validator;
  final int maxLines;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return TextFormField(
      controller: controller,
      keyboardType: keyboardType,
      validator: validator,
      maxLines: maxLines,
      style: const TextStyle(
        color: GardenTheme.ink,
        fontSize: 14,
        fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
      ),
      decoration: _inputDecoration(label, hintText: hintText),
    );
  }
}

class _DateButton extends StatelessWidget {
  const _DateButton({
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  final String label;
  final String value;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return InkWell(
      onTap: onTap,
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      child: InputDecorator(
        decoration: _inputDecoration(label),
        child: Text(
          value,
          style: const TextStyle(
            color: GardenTheme.ink,
            fontSize: 14,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

InputDecoration _inputDecoration(String label, {String? hintText}) {
  return InputDecoration(
    labelText: label.toUpperCase(),
    hintText: hintText,
    labelStyle: const TextStyle(
      color: GardenTheme.muted,
      fontSize: 11,
      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
      letterSpacing: 0.8,
    ),
    filled: true,
    fillColor: GardenTheme.paper,
    contentPadding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 12),
    enabledBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.border),
    ),
    focusedBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.ink, width: 1.4),
    ),
    errorBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.bad),
    ),
    focusedErrorBorder: OutlineInputBorder(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      borderSide: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.bad, width: 1.4),
    ),
  );
}

String _shortDate(DateTime date) {
  return '${date.day.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}/${date.month.toString().padLeft(2, '0')}';
}

class EditSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const EditSeedlingDialog({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<EditSeedlingDialog> createState() => _EditSeedlingDialogState();
}

class _EditSeedlingDialogState extends State<EditSeedlingDialog> {
  final formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();

  late SeedCatalogItem selected;
  late DateTime sowDate;
  String? selectedBedId;

  late final TextEditingController varietyController;
  late final TextEditingController trayTypeController;
  late final TextEditingController trayCountController;
  late final TextEditingController locationController;
  late final TextEditingController notesController;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    selected = SeedCatalog.byKey(widget.seedling.seedKey);
    sowDate = widget.seedling.sowDate;
    selectedBedId = widget.seedling.bedId;

    varietyController = TextEditingController(text: widget.seedling.variety);
    trayTypeController = TextEditingController(text: widget.seedling.trayType);
    trayCountController = TextEditingController(
      text: widget.seedling.trayCount.toString(),
    );
    locationController = TextEditingController(text: widget.seedling.location);
    notesController = TextEditingController(text: widget.seedling.notes);
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    varietyController.dispose();
    trayTypeController.dispose();
    trayCountController.dispose();
    locationController.dispose();
    notesController.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Dialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        side: const BorderSide(color: GardenTheme.border),
      ),
      child: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: BoxConstraints(
          maxWidth: 620,
          maxHeight: MediaQuery.of(context).size.height * 0.88,
        ),
        child: SingleChildScrollView(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(22),
          child: Form(
            key: formKey,
            child: Column(
              mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                const Text(
                  'Edit Seedling',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.ink,
                    fontSize: 24,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    letterSpacing: -0.3,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 6),
                const Text(
                  'Update crop, sow date, batch details, location, bed assignment, and notes.',
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 13,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 18),
                DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                  initialValue: selected.key,
                  isExpanded: true,
                  decoration: _inputDecoration('SEED TYPE'),
                  items: [
                    for (final item in SeedCatalog.items)
                      DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: item.key,
                        child: Text('${item.emoji} ${item.cropName}'),
                      ),
                  ],
                  onChanged: (value) {
                    final key = value ?? selected.key;
                    setState(() {
                      selected = SeedCatalog.byKey(key);
                    });
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Variety',
                  controller: varietyController,
                  hintText: selected.varieties.isEmpty
                      ? 'Optional'
                      : selected.varieties.take(3).join(', '),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [
                          _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                          const SizedBox(height: 12),
                          _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(
                          child: _DateButton(
                            label: 'Sow date',
                            value: _shortDate(sowDate),
                            onTap: _pickSowDate,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Tray type',
                            controller: trayTypeController,
                            validator: _required,
                          ),
                        ),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(
                          child: _TextField(
                            label: 'Count',
                            controller: trayCountController,
                            keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
                            validator: _positiveInt,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                LayoutBuilder(
                  builder: (context, constraints) {
                    final stacked = constraints.maxWidth < 560;

                    final location = _TextField(
                      label: 'Location',
                      controller: locationController,
                      validator: _required,
                    );

                    final bed = DropdownButtonFormField<String?>(
                      initialValue: selectedBedId,
                      isExpanded: true,
                      decoration: _inputDecoration('ASSIGNED BED'),
                      items: [
                        const DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                          value: null,
                          child: Text('No bed assigned'),
                        ),
                        for (final bed in widget.beds)
                          DropdownMenuItem<String?>(
                            value: bed.id,
                            child: Text(
                              bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                                  ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                                  : bed.name.trim(),
                              overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                            ),
                          ),
                      ],
                      onChanged: (value) {
                        setState(() {
                          selectedBedId = value;
                        });
                      },
                    );

                    if (stacked) {
                      return Column(
                        children: [location, const SizedBox(height: 12), bed],
                      );
                    }

                    return Row(
                      children: [
                        Expanded(child: location),
                        const SizedBox(width: 12),
                        Expanded(child: bed),
                      ],
                    );
                  },
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 12),
                _TextField(
                  label: 'Notes',
                  controller: notesController,
                  maxLines: 3,
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 14),
                Container(
                  width: double.infinity,
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: GardenTheme.paper,
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
                    border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
                  ),
                  child: Text(
                    '${selected.tip} Germination: ${selected.germinationMinDays}-${selected.germinationMaxDays} days. Transplant: ${selected.transplantMinDays}-${selected.transplantMaxDays} days.',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.muted,
                      fontSize: 12,
                      height: 1.35,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 22),
                Wrap(
                  spacing: 10,
                  runSpacing: 10,
                  alignment: WrapAlignment.end,
                  children: [
                    TextButton(
                      onPressed: () {
                        Navigator.of(context).pop();
                      },
                      child: const Text('Cancel'),
                    ),
                    FilledButton(
                      onPressed: _submit,
                      child: const Text('Save changes'),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Future<void> _pickSowDate() async {
    final result = await showDatePicker(
      context: context,
      initialDate: sowDate,
      firstDate: DateTime.now().subtract(const Duration(days: 365)),
      lastDate: DateTime.now().add(const Duration(days: 30)),
    );

    if (result == null) return;

    setState(() {
      sowDate = result;
    });
  }

  void _submit() {
    if (!formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;

    Navigator.of(context).pop(
      Seedling(
        id: widget.seedling.id,
        seedKey: selected.key,
        cropName: selected.cropName,
        emoji: selected.emoji,
        category: selected.category,
        variety: varietyController.text.trim(),
        sowDate: sowDate,
        trayType: trayTypeController.text.trim(),
        trayCount: int.tryParse(trayCountController.text.trim()) ?? 1,
        location: locationController.text.trim(),
        notes: notesController.text.trim(),
        bedId: selectedBedId,
        lastWateredAt: widget.seedling.lastWateredAt,
        lastFedAt: widget.seedling.lastFedAt,
        transplantedAt: widget.seedling.transplantedAt,
      ),
    );
  }

  String? _required(String? value) {
    if (value == null || value.trim().isEmpty) {
      return 'Required';
    }

    return null;
  }

  String? _positiveInt(String? value) {
    final parsed = int.tryParse(value ?? '');

    if (parsed == null) return 'Enter a number';
    if (parsed < 1) return 'Minimum 1';

    return null;
  }
}

class TransplantSeedlingDialog extends StatefulWidget {
  const TransplantSeedlingDialog({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<TransplantSeedlingDialog> createState() =>
      _TransplantSeedlingDialogState();
}

class _TransplantSeedlingDialogState extends State<TransplantSeedlingDialog> {
  String? selectedBedId;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    final existingBedId = widget.seedling.bedId;

    if (existingBedId != null &&
        widget.beds.any((bed) => bed.id == existingBedId)) {
      selectedBedId = existingBedId;
    } else if (widget.beds.isNotEmpty) {
      selectedBedId = widget.beds.first.id;
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AlertDialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      title: const Text('Transplant to Bed'),
      content: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 460),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Row(
              children: [
                Text(
                  widget.seedling.emoji,
                  style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 30),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 10),
                Expanded(
                  child: Text(
                    widget.seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                        ? widget.seedling.cropName
                        : '${widget.seedling.cropName} - ${widget.seedling.variety}',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.ink,
                      fontSize: 16,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            const Text(
              'Choose the bed this seedling was transplanted into. The crop name will be added to that bed if it is not already listed.',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                height: 1.35,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              initialValue: selectedBedId,
              isExpanded: true,
              decoration: _inputDecoration('TARGET BED'),
              items: [
                for (final bed in widget.beds)
                  DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                    value: bed.id,
                    child: Text(
                      bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                          : '${bed.name} (${bed.zone})',
                      overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                    ),
                  ),
              ],
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedBedId = value;
                });
              },
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      actions: [
        TextButton(
          onPressed: () {
            Navigator.of(context).pop();
          },
          child: const Text('Cancel'),
        ),
        FilledButton.icon(
          onPressed: selectedBedId == null
              ? null
              : () {
                  Navigator.of(context).pop(selectedBedId);
                },
          icon: const Icon(Icons.task_alt),
          label: const Text('Transplant'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

class TransplantSeedlingResult {
  const TransplantSeedlingResult({
    required this.bedId,
    required this.addCropBlockToMap,
  });

  final String bedId;
  final bool addCropBlockToMap;
}

class TransplantSeedlingDialogV2 extends StatefulWidget {
  const TransplantSeedlingDialogV2({
    super.key,
    required this.seedling,
    required this.beds,
  });

  final Seedling seedling;
  final List<Bed> beds;

  @override
  State<TransplantSeedlingDialogV2> createState() =>
      _TransplantSeedlingDialogV2State();
}

class _TransplantSeedlingDialogV2State
    extends State<TransplantSeedlingDialogV2> {
  String? selectedBedId;
  bool addCropBlockToMap = true;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    final existingBedId = widget.seedling.bedId;

    if (existingBedId != null &&
        widget.beds.any((bed) => bed.id == existingBedId)) {
      selectedBedId = existingBedId;
    } else if (widget.beds.isNotEmpty) {
      selectedBedId = widget.beds.first.id;
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AlertDialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      title: const Text('Transplant to Bed'),
      content: ConstrainedBox(
        constraints: const BoxConstraints(maxWidth: 480),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Row(
              children: [
                Text(
                  widget.seedling.emoji,
                  style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 30),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 10),
                Expanded(
                  child: Text(
                    widget.seedling.variety.trim().isEmpty
                        ? widget.seedling.cropName
                        : '${widget.seedling.cropName} - ${widget.seedling.variety}',
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: GardenTheme.ink,
                      fontSize: 16,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            const Text(
              'Choose the bed this seedling was transplanted into. The crop name will be added to that bed. If map placement is enabled, a crop block will be added inside the bed on the map.',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                height: 1.35,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 14),
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              initialValue: selectedBedId,
              isExpanded: true,
              decoration: _inputDecoration('TARGET BED'),
              items: [
                for (final bed in widget.beds)
                  DropdownMenuItem<String>(
                    value: bed.id,
                    child: Text(
                      bed.name.trim().isEmpty
                          ? 'Bed ${bed.number}'
                          : '${bed.name} (${bed.zone})',
                      overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                    ),
                  ),
              ],
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedBedId = value;
                });
              },
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 12),
            CheckboxListTile(
              value: addCropBlockToMap,
              dense: true,
              contentPadding: EdgeInsets.zero,
              controlAffinity: ListTileControlAffinity.leading,
              title: const Text(
                'Add crop block to map',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: GardenTheme.ink,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
                ),
              ),
              subtitle: const Text(
                'Creates a visible crop row/block inside the selected bed.',
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: GardenTheme.muted,
                  fontSize: 12,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                ),
              ),
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  addCropBlockToMap = value ?? true;
                });
              },
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      actions: [
        TextButton(
          onPressed: () {
            Navigator.of(context).pop();
          },
          child: const Text('Cancel'),
        ),
        FilledButton.icon(
          onPressed: selectedBedId == null
              ? null
              : () {
                  Navigator.of(context).pop(
                    TransplantSeedlingResult(
                      bedId: selectedBedId!,
                      addCropBlockToMap: addCropBlockToMap,
                    ),
                  );
                },
          icon: const Icon(Icons.task_alt),
          label: const Text('Transplant'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

import '../../../../core/theme/garden_theme.dart';

class ShortcutsHelpButton extends StatelessWidget {
  const ShortcutsHelpButton({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return IconButton(
      tooltip: 'Keyboard shortcuts',
      icon: const Icon(Icons.keyboard_alt_outlined),
      color: GardenTheme.muted,
      onPressed: () {
        showDialog<void>(
          context: context,
          builder: (context) {
            return const ShortcutsHelpDialog();
          },
        );
      },
    );
  }
}

class ShortcutsHelpDialog extends StatelessWidget {
  const ShortcutsHelpDialog({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AlertDialog(
      backgroundColor: GardenTheme.panel,
      title: const Text('Keyboard Shortcuts'),
      content: const SizedBox(
        width: 420,
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            _ShortcutRow(keys: 'Ctrl + S', action: 'Save project'),
            _ShortcutRow(keys: 'Ctrl + Z', action: 'Undo'),
            _ShortcutRow(keys: 'Ctrl + Y', action: 'Redo'),
            _ShortcutRow(keys: 'F', action: 'Fit map to screen'),
            _ShortcutRow(keys: '0', action: 'Reset zoom to 100%'),
            _ShortcutRow(keys: 'Esc', action: 'Close open panel later'),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      actions: [
        TextButton(
          onPressed: () {
            Navigator.of(context).pop();
          },
          child: Text('Close'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

class _ShortcutRow extends StatelessWidget {
  const _ShortcutRow({required this.keys, required this.action});

  final String keys;
  final String action;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 7),
      child: Row(

          Container(

              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
              border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
            ),
            child: Text(
              keys,
              textAlign: TextAlign.center,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.ink,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w900,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: Text(
              action,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 13,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

import '../../../../core/theme/garden_theme.dart';
import '../../services/spray_conditions_service.dart';

class SprayConditionsWidget extends StatefulWidget {
  const SprayConditionsWidget({
    super.key,
    this.compactMode = false,
    this.latitude = SprayConditionsService.defaultLatitude,
    this.longitude = SprayConditionsService.defaultLongitude,
  });

  final double latitude;
  final double longitude;
  final bool compactMode;

  @override
  State<SprayConditionsWidget> createState() => _SprayConditionsWidgetState();
}

class _SprayConditionsWidgetState extends State<SprayConditionsWidget> {
  final SprayConditionsService service = const SprayConditionsService();

  late Future<SprayConditions> conditionsFuture;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    conditionsFuture = _load();
  }

  @override
  void didUpdateWidget(covariant SprayConditionsWidget oldWidget) {
    super.didUpdateWidget(oldWidget);

    if (oldWidget.latitude != widget.latitude ||
        oldWidget.longitude != widget.longitude) {
      conditionsFuture = _load();
    }
  }

  Future<SprayConditions> _load() {
    return service.fetchCurrent(
      latitude: widget.latitude,
      longitude: widget.longitude,
    );
  }

  void _refresh() {
    setState(() {
      conditionsFuture = _load();
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return FutureBuilder<SprayConditions>(
      future: conditionsFuture,
      builder: (context, snapshot) {
        if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
          return const _SprayLoading();
        }

        if (snapshot.hasError) {
          return _SprayError(
            message: snapshot.error.toString(),
            onRetry: _refresh,
          );
        }

        final conditions = snapshot.data;

        if (conditions == null) {
          return _SprayError(
            message: 'No spray condition data available.',
            onRetry: _refresh,
          );
        }

        return _SprayContent(conditions: conditions, onRefresh: _refresh);
      },
    );
  }
}

class _SprayLoading extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SprayLoading();

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return _SprayShell(
      child: const Row(
        children: [
          SizedBox(
            width: 18,
            height: 18,
            child: CircularProgressIndicator(strokeWidth: 2),
          ),
          SizedBox(width: 10),
          Text(
            'Loading spray conditions...',
            style: TextStyle(
              color: GardenTheme.muted,
              fontSize: 12,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _SprayError extends StatelessWidget {
  const _SprayError({required this.message, required this.onRetry});

  final String message;
  final VoidCallback onRetry;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return _SprayShell(
      child: Row(
        children: [
          const Icon(Icons.warning_amber, color: GardenTheme.warn, size: 18),
          const SizedBox(width: 10),
          Expanded(
            child: Text(
              message,
              maxLines: 2,
              overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: GardenTheme.muted,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          TextButton(onPressed: onRetry, child: const Text('Retry')),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _SprayHeader extends StatelessWidget {

class _SprayShell extends StatelessWidget {

  final Widget child;

  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      constraints: const BoxConstraints(minHeight: 0),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),

        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(18),
        border: Border.all(color: GardenTheme.border),
        boxShadow: const [

            blurRadius: 16,
            offset: Offset(0, 5),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: child,
    );
  }

Color _suitabilityColor(SpraySuitability suitability) {
  switch (suitability) {
    case SpraySuitability.good:
      return GardenTheme.good;
    case SpraySuitability.caution:
      return GardenTheme.warn;
    case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
      return GardenTheme.bad;
  }
}

Color _suitabilityBackground(SpraySuitability suitability) {
  switch (suitability) {
    case SpraySuitability.good:
      return const Color(0xFFEEF8F0);
    case SpraySuitability.caution:
      return const Color(0xFFFFF3E5);
    case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
      return const Color(0xFFFFF0EE);
  }
}

IconData _suitabilityIcon(SpraySuitability suitability) {
  switch (suitability) {
    case SpraySuitability.good:
      return Icons.check_circle_outline;
    case SpraySuitability.caution:
      return Icons.warning_amber_rounded;
    case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
      return Icons.block_outlined;
  }
}

String _suitabilityTitle(SpraySuitability suitability) {
  switch (suitability) {
    case SpraySuitability.good:
      return 'Good spray window';
    case SpraySuitability.caution:
      return 'Spray with caution';
    case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
      return 'Do not spray';
  }
}

String _suitabilityChipLabel(SpraySuitability suitability) {
  switch (suitability) {
    case SpraySuitability.good:
      return 'GOOD';
    case SpraySuitability.caution:
      return 'CAUTION';
    case SpraySuitability.noSpray:
      return 'NO SPRAY';
  }
}

Color _windColor(SprayConditions conditions) {
  if (conditions.windSpeedKmh >= 18 || conditions.windGustKmh >= 28) {
    return GardenTheme.bad;
  }
  if (conditions.windSpeedKmh >= 12 || conditions.windGustKmh >= 20) {
    return GardenTheme.warn;
  }
  return GardenTheme.good;
}

Color _rainColor(SprayConditions conditions) {
  return conditions.precipitationMm > 0.2 ? GardenTheme.bad : GardenTheme.good;
}

Color _humidityColor(int humidity) {
  if (humidity >= 90 || humidity <= 35) return GardenTheme.warn;
  return GardenTheme.good;
}

Color _temperatureColor(double temperatureC) {
  if (temperatureC >= 29) return GardenTheme.bad;
  if (temperatureC >= 25) return GardenTheme.warn;
  return GardenTheme.good;
}

Color _uvColor(double uvIndex) {
  if (uvIndex >= 8) return GardenTheme.bad;
  if (uvIndex >= 6) return GardenTheme.warn;
  return GardenTheme.good;
}

String _humidityCaption(int humidity) {
  if (humidity >= 90) return 'Very humid';
  if (humidity <= 35) return 'Very dry';
  return 'Suitable';
}

String _temperatureCaption(double temperatureC) {
  if (temperatureC >= 29) return 'Too hot';
  if (temperatureC >= 25) return 'Warm';
  return 'Suitable';
}

String _uvCaption(double uvIndex) {
  if (uvIndex >= 8) return 'Very high';
  if (uvIndex >= 6) return 'High';
  return 'Suitable';
}

import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

import '../../../../core/models/bed.dart';
import '../../../../core/theme/garden_theme.dart';

class SummaryCards extends StatelessWidget {
  const SummaryCards({
    super.key,
    required this.beds,
    required this.overlapCount,
  });

  final List<Bed> beds;
  final int overlapCount;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final totalBeds = beds.length;

    final plantedCrops = beds
        .expand((bed) => bed.crops)
        .where((crop) => crop.trim().isNotEmpty)
        .toSet()
        .length;

    final needsAttention = beds
        .where((bed) => bed.status != BedStatus.ok)
        .length;

    final totalArea = beds.fold<double>(
      0,
      (sum, bed) => sum + bed.width * bed.height,
    );

    return SizedBox(
      height: 108,
      child: ListView(
        scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
        children: [
          SummaryCard(
            label: 'Total Beds',
            value: totalBeds.toString(),
            sublabel: 'Active layout cards',
            accentColor: GardenTheme.ink,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          SummaryCard(
            label: 'Planted Crops',
            value: plantedCrops.toString(),
            sublabel: 'Unique crop labels',
            accentColor: GardenTheme.good,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          SummaryCard(
            label: 'Needs Attention',
            value: needsAttention.toString(),
            sublabel: 'Warning, issue, or hold',
            accentColor: needsAttention == 0
                ? GardenTheme.good
                : GardenTheme.warn,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          SummaryCard(
            label: 'Layout Issues',
            value: overlapCount.toString(),
            sublabel: overlapCount == 0
                ? 'No overlapping beds'
                : 'Overlapping bed warnings',
            accentColor: overlapCount == 0 ? GardenTheme.good : GardenTheme.bad,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          SummaryCard(
            label: 'Garden Area',
            value: '${totalArea.toStringAsFixed(0)} mÂ²',
            sublabel: 'Total planned bed area',
            accentColor: GardenTheme.hold,
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class SummaryCard extends StatelessWidget {
  const SummaryCard({
    super.key,
    required this.label,
    required this.value,
    required this.sublabel,
    required this.accentColor,
  });

  final String label;
  final String value;
  final String sublabel;
  final Color accentColor;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      width: 220,
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 13),
      decoration: GardenTheme.cardDecoration(
        background: GardenTheme.panel,
        borderColor: GardenTheme.border,
        radius: 14,
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Container(
            width: 5,
            height: double.infinity,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: accentColor,
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(999),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 13),
          Expanded(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  label.toUpperCase(),
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 10,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
                    letterSpacing: 0.9,
                  ),
                ),
                const SizedBox(height: 7),
                Text(
                  value,
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: accentColor,
                    fontSize: 24,
                    height: 1,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w800,
                  ),
                ),
                const Spacer(),
                Text(
                  sublabel,
                  maxLines: 1,
                  overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: GardenTheme.muted,
                    fontSize: 11,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';

@immutable
class ViewOptions {
  const ViewOptions({
    this.dashboardExpanded = true,
    this.gridVisible = true,
    this.labelsVisible = true,
    this.cropRowsVisible = true,
    this.mapInstructionsVisible = true,
  });

  final bool dashboardExpanded;
  final bool gridVisible;
  final bool labelsVisible;
  final bool cropRowsVisible;
  final bool mapInstructionsVisible;

  ViewOptions copyWith({
    bool? dashboardExpanded,
    bool? gridVisible,
    bool? labelsVisible,
    bool? cropRowsVisible,
    bool? mapInstructionsVisible,
  }) {
    return ViewOptions(
      dashboardExpanded: dashboardExpanded ?? this.dashboardExpanded,
      gridVisible: gridVisible ?? this.gridVisible,
      labelsVisible: labelsVisible ?? this.labelsVisible,
      cropRowsVisible: cropRowsVisible ?? this.cropRowsVisible,
      mapInstructionsVisible:
          mapInstructionsVisible ?? this.mapInstructionsVisible,
    );
  }
}

FILE: lib\models\bed.dart
------------------------------------------------------------

import 'crop_placement.dart';

enum BedStatus { ok, warning, bad, hold }

class Bed {
  const Bed({
    required this.id,
    required this.number,
    required this.name,
    required this.x,
    required this.y,
    required this.width,
    required this.height,
    required this.zone,
    required this.status,
    required this.healthPercent,
    required this.crops,
    this.cropPlacements = const [],
  });

  final String id;
  final int number;
  final String name;

  /// Position on the garden canvas, measured in meters.
  final double x;
  final double y;

  /// Bed size, measured in meters.
  final double width;
  final double height;

  final String zone;
  final BedStatus status;
  final double healthPercent;
  final List<String> crops;

  /// Manual crop icon placements inside this bed.
  ///
  /// Each placement uses bed-local coordinates:
  /// x = meters from bed left edge
  /// y = meters from bed top edge
  final List<CropPlacement> cropPlacements;

  Bed copyWith({
    String? id,
    int? number,
    String? name,
    double? x,
    double? y,
    double? width,
    double? height,
    String? zone,
    BedStatus? status,
    double? healthPercent,
    List<String>? crops,
    List<CropPlacement>? cropPlacements,
  }) {
    return Bed(
      id: id ?? this.id,
      number: number ?? this.number,
      name: name ?? this.name,
      x: x ?? this.x,
      y: y ?? this.y,
      width: width ?? this.width,
      height: height ?? this.height,
      zone: zone ?? this.zone,
      status: status ?? this.status,
      healthPercent: healthPercent ?? this.healthPercent,
      crops: crops ?? this.crops,
      cropPlacements: cropPlacements ?? this.cropPlacements,
    );
  }

  Map<String, dynamic> toJson() {
    return {
      'id': id,
      'x': x,
      'y': y,
      'width': width,
      'height': height,
      'number': number,
      'name': name,
      'zone': zone,
      'status': status.name,
      'healthPercent': healthPercent,
      'crops': crops,
      'cropPlacements': cropPlacements
          .map((placement) => placement.toJson())
          .toList(),
    };
  }

  factory Bed.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic> json) {
    return Bed(
      id: json['id']?.toString() ?? '',
      x: _readDouble(json['x']),
      y: _readDouble(json['y']),
      width: _readDouble(json['width']),
      height: _readDouble(json['height']),
      number: _readInt(json['number']),
      name: json['name']?.toString() ?? 'Untitled Bed',
      zone: json['zone']?.toString() ?? 'Main Garden',
      status: _readStatus(json['status']),
      healthPercent: _readDouble(json['healthPercent'], fallback: 1.0),
      crops: _readStringList(json['crops']),
      cropPlacements: _readCropPlacements(json['cropPlacements']),
    );
  }

  static BedStatus _readStatus(Object? value) {
    final raw = value?.toString();

    for (final status in BedStatus.values) {
      if (status.name == raw) {
        return status;
      }
    }

    return BedStatus.ok;
  }

  static List<String> _readStringList(Object? value) {
    if (value is! List) return const [];

    return value
        .map((item) => item.toString().trim())
        .where((item) => item.isNotEmpty)
        .toList();
  }

  static List<CropPlacement> _readCropPlacements(Object? value) {
    if (value is! List) return const [];

    return value
        .whereType<Map>()
        .map((item) => CropPlacement.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic>.from(item)))
        .where((placement) => placement.id.trim().isNotEmpty)
        .toList();
  }

  static double _readDouble(Object? value, {double fallback = 0}) {
    if (value is num) return value.toDouble();
    if (value is String) return double.tryParse(value) ?? fallback;
    return fallback;
  }

  static int _readInt(Object? value, {int fallback = 0}) {
    if (value is int) return value;
    if (value is num) return value.toInt();
    if (value is String) return int.tryParse(value) ?? fallback;
    return fallback;
  }
}

FILE: lib\models\garden_project.dart
------------------------------------------------------------

import 'bed.dart';

class GardenProject {
  final String id;
  final String name;
  final double widthMeters;
  final double heightMeters;
  final List<Bed> beds;
  final DateTime updatedAt;

  const GardenProject({
    required this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.widthMeters,
    required this.heightMeters,
    required this.beds,
    required this.updatedAt,
  });

  factory GardenProject.demo() {
    return GardenProject(
      id: 'demo-project',
      name: 'Blenheim Garden Plan',
      widthMeters: 30,
      heightMeters: 18,
      updatedAt: DateTime.now(),
      beds: const [
        Bed(
          id: '1',
          number: 1,
          name: 'Strawberry Bed',
          x: 2,
          y: 2,
          width: 8,
          height: 4,
          zone: 'Berry Zone',
          status: BedStatus.ok,
          healthPercent: 0.9,
          crops: ['Strawberries'],
        ),
        Bed(
          id: '2',
          number: 2,
          name: 'Raspberry + Strawberry Bed',
          x: 2,
          y: 7,
          width: 8,
          height: 4,
          zone: 'Berry Zone',
          status: BedStatus.warning,
          healthPercent: 0.7,
          crops: ['Raspberries', 'Strawberries'],
        ),
        Bed(
          id: '3',
          number: 3,
          name: 'Broccoli Bed',
          x: 12,
          y: 4,
          width: 6,
          height: 4,
          zone: 'Main Garden',
          status: BedStatus.ok,
          healthPercent: 0.85,
          crops: ['Broccoli'],
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  GardenProject copyWith({
    String? id,
    String? name,
    double? widthMeters,
    double? heightMeters,
    List<Bed>? beds,
    DateTime? updatedAt,
  }) {
    return GardenProject(
      id: id ?? this.id,
      name: name ?? this.name,
      widthMeters: widthMeters ?? this.widthMeters,
      heightMeters: heightMeters ?? this.heightMeters,
      beds: beds ?? this.beds,
      updatedAt: updatedAt ?? this.updatedAt,
    );
  }

  Map<String, dynamic> toJson() {
    return {
      'id': id,
      'name': name,
      'widthMeters': widthMeters,
      'heightMeters': heightMeters,
      'beds': beds.map((bed) => bed.toJson()).toList(),
      'updatedAt': updatedAt.toIso8601String(),
    };
  }

  factory GardenProject.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic> json) {
    return GardenProject(
      id: json['id'] as String? ?? 'project',
      name: json['name'] as String? ?? 'Untitled Garden Plan',
      widthMeters: _toDouble(json['widthMeters'], fallback: 30),
      heightMeters: _toDouble(json['heightMeters'], fallback: 18),
      beds: _bedsFromJson(json['beds']),
      updatedAt: _dateTimeFromJson(json['updatedAt']),
    );
  }

  static List<Bed> _bedsFromJson(dynamic value) {
    if (value is List) {
      return value
          .whereType<Map>()
          .map((item) => Bed.fromJson(Map<String, dynamic>.from(item)))
          .toList();
    }

    return const [];
  }

  static DateTime _dateTimeFromJson(dynamic value) {
    if (value is String) {
      return DateTime.tryParse(value) ?? DateTime.now();
    }

    return DateTime.now();
  }

  static double _toDouble(dynamic value, {double fallback = 0.0}) {
    if (value is double) return value;
    if (value is int) return value.toDouble();
    if (value is String) return double.tryParse(value) ?? fallback;

    return fallback;
  }
}
